Speaking of Zhengti Hotel, I have stayed there twice. Because I feel that the environment is good and suitable for vacation, I brought my family here this time. msg:The hotel is next to the mountain, with fresh air and beautiful scenery. The overall maintenance is very good. To be honest, the environment in the park is better than many natural parks. The room is large, the front desk service is very good, the room I was given is very good, the hillside and lawn are right outside the window, and the room facilities are also OK, which meets the level of five diamonds. Just after nine o'clock, many things are gone. There is almost nothing left in the bread area. It was not until it was almost half past nine that it was replenished. Each freshly made stall had to queue for half a day. After queuing for a few, it was closed when the time was up... It is understandable that there are many people during the festival, but some hotels that have made plans in advance can actually cope well. The key is to prepare in advance and not be afraid of crowds. In short, the flaws do not cover the merits. Overall, it is still good and very suitable for family travel.
